You are a leading expert in constructing dynamic ecosystem models. You always use robust ecological theory to construct your models, which will be used for predicting future ecosystem states given data on initial conditions. Please create a Template Model Builder model for the following topic:The dynamical behaviour of a simple plankton population model, which explicitly simulates the concentrations of nutrient (N), phytoplankton (P) and zooplankton (Z) in the oceanic mixed layer. Start by writing intention.txt, in which you provide a concise summary of the ecological functioning of the model. In model.cpp, write your TMB model with the following important considerations:

1. ECOLOGICAL PROCESSES:
- Consider multiple forms of resource limitation (e.g., saturating functions, threshold effects)
- Include process-specific efficiencies where biologically relevant
- Think about how environmental conditions might modify rates
- Consider indirect effects and feedback loops between components
- Use functional responses that capture observed biological behaviors

2. NUMERICAL STABILITY:
- Always use small constants (e.g., Type(1e-8)) to prevent division by zero
- Use smooth transitions instead of hard cutoffs in equations
- Bound parameters within biologically meaningful ranges using smooth penalties rather than hard constraints
  (and propose numeric lower/upper bounds per parameter when applicable; see parameters.json spec below)

3. LIKELIHOOD CALCULATION:
- Always include observations in the likelihood calculation, don't skip any based on conditions
- Use fixed minimum standard deviations to prevent numerical issues when data values are small
- Consider log-transforming data if it spans multiple orders of magnitude
- Use appropriate error distributions (e.g., lognormal for strictly positive data)

4. MODEL STRUCTURE:
- Include comments after each line explaining the parameters (including their units and how to determine their values)
- Provide a numbered list of descriptions for the equations
- Ensure all _pred variables are included in the reporting section and called using REPORT()
- Use '_pred' suffix for model predictions corresponding to '_dat' observations. Use the same _dat names as are found in the data file. Use the exact same time variable name as is provided in the first column of the datafile.
- IMPORTANT: Never use current time step values of response variables (variables ending in '_dat') in prediction calculations. Only use values from previous time steps to avoid data leakage.
- INITIAL CONDITIONS: Initialize your prediction vectors with the first data point using **name**_dat(0). For example: var1_pred(0) = var1_dat(0); var2_pred(0) = var2_dat(0); var3_pred(0) = var3_dat(0). This ensures initial conditions are drawn directly from the observed data rather than being optimization parameters.

For the parameters.json file, please structure it as an array of parameter objects, where each parameter object must include the following fields:
- parameter: The name of the parameter matching the model.cpp
- value: The initial value for the parameter
- description: A clear description of what the parameter represents, including units
- source: Where the initial value comes from. IMPORTANT: If the source contains the word 'literature', this will automatically trigger downstream literature searches using Semantic Scholar and other academic databases to find citations and refine parameter values. Use 'literature' only when you want the system to search for academic papers. Use 'initial estimate' for parameters that are unlikely to have reported values in the literature.
- import_type: Should be 'PARAMETER' for model parameters, or 'DATA_VECTOR'/'DATA_SCALAR' for data inputs
- priority: A number indicating the optimization priority (1 for highest priority parameters to optimize first)
- lower_bound (optional): Suggested biological lower bound as a number, or null if not applicable
- upper_bound (optional): Suggested biological upper bound as a number, or null if not applicable

Example structure:
{
  "parameters": [
    {
      "parameter": "growth_rate",
      "value": 0.5,
      "units": "dimensionsless | year ^-1",
      "description": "Intrinsic growth rate (year^-1)",
      "source": "literature",
      "import_type": "PARAMETER",
      "priority": 1,
      "lower_bound": 0.0,
      "upper_bound": null
    }
  ]
}

Of course. As an expert in dynamic ecosystem modeling, I will construct a robust Nutrient-Phytoplankton-Zooplankton (NPZ) model based on established ecological principles.                                                 

Here is a summary of the model's ecological functioning, followed by the TMB model implementation in C++ and the corresponding parameter file.                                                                              

POPULATIONS/POPULATION_0021/INDIVIDUAL_PVV9N9FN/intention.txt                                                                                                                                                               

                                                                                                                                                                                                                            
 @@ -0,0 +1,10 @@                                                                                                                                                                                                           
 +This model simulates the dynamics of a simple marine food web involving nutrients (N), phytoplankton (P), and zooplankton (Z) in a closed system, such as the oceanic mixed layer.                                        
 +                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
 +The model is based on the following interactions:                                                                                                                                                                         
 +1. Phytoplankton growth is driven by the uptake of dissolved nutrients, following Michaelis-Menten kinetics, which means growth rate saturates at high nutrient concentrations.                                           
 +2. Zooplankton graze on phytoplankton, with a Holling Type II functional response, where consumption rate saturates as phytoplankton become abundant.                                                                     
 +3. A fraction of the grazed phytoplankton is assimilated by zooplankton for growth, while the rest is egested.                                                                                                            
 +4. Both phytoplankton and zooplankton populations experience loss through a linear mortality term.                                                                                                                        
 +5. Dead organic matter from mortality and zooplankton egestion is remineralized back into the dissolved nutrient pool, closing the nutrient loop.                                                                         
 +                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
 +This structure creates a dynamic feedback system where predator-prey oscillations and nutrient cycling can be observed. The model is designed to be fitted to time-series data of N, P, and Z concentrations.

POPULATIONS/POPULATION_0021/INDIVIDUAL_PVV9N9FN/model.cpp                                                                                                                                                                   

                                                                                                                                                                                                                            
 @@ -0,0 +1,147 @@                                                                                                                                                                                                          
 +#include <TMB.hpp>                                                                                                                                                                                                        
 +                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
 +template<class Type>                                                                                                                                                                                                      
 +Type objective_function<Type>::operator() ()                                                                                                                                                                              
 +{                                                                                                                                                                                                                         
 +  // ------------------------------------------------------------------------                                                                                                                                             
 +  // DATA                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
 +  // ------------------------------------------------------------------------                                                                                                                                             
 +                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
 +  // These variable names must match the 'parameter' field in parameters.json                                                                                                                                             
 +  DATA_VECTOR(Time_days); // Time vector (days)                                                                                                                                                                           
 +  DATA_VECTOR(N_dat);     // Observed Nutrient concentration (g C m^-3)                                                                                                                                                   
 +  DATA_VECTOR(P_dat);     // Observed Phytoplankton concentration (g C m^-3)                                                                                                                                              
 +  DATA_VECTOR(Z_dat);     // Observed Zooplankton concentration (g C m^-3)                                                                                                                                                
 +                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
 +  // ------------------------------------------------------------------------                                                                                                                                             
 +  // PARAMETERS                                                                                                                                                                                                           
 +  // ------------------------------------------------------------------------                                                                                                                                             
 +                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
 +  // These variable names must match the 'parameter' field in parameters.json                                                                                                                                             
 +  PARAMETER(V_max);   // Maximum phytoplankton uptake rate (day^-1)                                                                                                                                                       
 +  PARAMETER(K_N);     // Nutrient uptake half-saturation constant (g C m^-3)                                                                                                                                              
 +  PARAMETER(mu_P);    // Phytoplankton mortality rate (day^-1)                                                                                                                                                            
 +  PARAMETER(I_max);   // Maximum zooplankton grazing rate (day^-1)                                                                                                                                                        
 +  PARAMETER(K_P);     // Grazing half-saturation constant (g C m^-3)                                                                                                                                                      
 +  PARAMETER(beta);    // Zooplankton assimilation efficiency (dimensionless)                                                                                                                                              
 +  PARAMETER(mu_Z);    // Zooplankton mortality rate (day^-1)                                                                                                                                                              
 +  PARAMETER(epsilon); // Remineralization rate (day^-1)                                                                                                                                                                   
 +                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
 +  // Observation error parameters                                                                                                                                                                                         
 +  PARAMETER(log_sigma_N); // Log of the standard deviation for Nutrient observations                                                                                                                                      
 +  PARAMETER(log_sigma_P); // Log of the standard deviation for Phytoplankton observations                                                                                                                                 
 +  PARAMETER(log_sigma_Z); // Log of the standard deviation for Zooplankton observations                                                                                                                                   
 +                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
 +  // ------------------------------------------------------------------------                                                                                                                                             
 +  // MODEL EQUATIONS                                                                                                                                                                                                      
 +  // ------------------------------------------------------------------------                                                                                                                                             
 +  //                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
 +  // 1. Nutrient Uptake (by Phytoplankton): V_max * (N / (K_N + N)) * P                                                                                                                                                   
 +  // 2. Grazing (of Phytoplankton by Zooplankton): I_max * (P / (K_P + P)) * Z                                                                                                                                            
 +  // 3. Phytoplankton Mortality: mu_P * P                                                                                                                                                                                 
 +  // 4. Zooplankton Mortality: mu_Z * Z                                                                                                                                                                                   
 +  // 5. Remineralization: epsilon * (Phytoplankton Mortality + Zooplankton Mortality + Unassimilated Grazing)                                                                                                             
 +  //                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
 +  // Resulting differential equations:                                                                                                                                                                                    
 +  // 6. dN/dt = -Uptake + Remineralization                                                                                                                                                                                
 +  // 7. dP/dt =  Uptake - Grazing - Phytoplankton Mortality                                                                                                                                                               
 +  // 8. dZ/dt =  (beta * Grazing) - Zooplankton Mortality                                                                                                                                                                 
 +  //                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
 +  // ------------------------------------------------------------------------                                                                                                                                             
 +                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
 +  Type nll = 0.0; // Initialize negative log-likelihood                                                                                                                                                                   
 +                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
 +  // ------------------------------------------------------------------------                                                                                                                                             
 +  // PARAMETER BOUNDS (using smooth penalties)                                                                                                                                                                            
 +  // ------------------------------------------------------------------------                                                                                                                                             
 +  Type penalty_weight = 100.0;                                                                                                                                                                                            
 +  if (V_max < 0.0)   nll += penalty_weight * pow(V_max - 0.0, 2);                                                                                                                                                         
 +  if (V_max > 5.0)   nll += penalty_weight * pow(V_max - 5.0, 2);                                                                                                                                                         
 +  if (K_N < 0.01)    nll += penalty_weight * pow(K_N - 0.01, 2);                                                                                                                                                          
 +  if (K_N > 1.0)     nll += penalty_weight * pow(K_N - 1.0, 2);                                                                                                                                                           
 +  if (mu_P < 0.0)    nll += penalty_weight * pow(mu_P - 0.0, 2);                                                                                                                                                          
 +  if (mu_P > 0.5)    nll += penalty_weight * pow(mu_P - 0.5, 2);                                                                                                                                                          
 +  if (I_max < 0.0)   nll += penalty_weight * pow(I_max - 0.0, 2);                                                                                                                                                         
 +  if (I_max > 2.0)   nll += penalty_weight * pow(I_max - 2.0, 2);                                                                                                                                                         
 +  if (K_P < 0.01)    nll += penalty_weight * pow(K_P - 0.01, 2);                                                                                                                                                          
 +  if (K_P > 1.0)     nll += penalty_weight * pow(K_P - 1.0, 2);                                                                                                                                                           
 +  if (beta < 0.1)    nll += penalty_weight * pow(beta - 0.1, 2);                                                                                                                                                          
 +  if (beta > 1.0)    nll += penalty_weight * pow(beta - 1.0, 2);                                                                                                                                                          
 +  if (mu_Z < 0.0)    nll += penalty_weight * pow(mu_Z - 0.0, 2);                                                                                                                                                          
 +  if (mu_Z > 0.5)    nll += penalty_weight * pow(mu_Z - 0.5, 2);                                                                                                                                                          
 +  if (epsilon < 0.0) nll += penalty_weight * pow(epsilon - 0.0, 2);                                                                                                                                                       
 +  if (epsilon > 1.0) nll += penalty_weight * pow(epsilon - 1.0, 2);                                                                                                                                                       
 +                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
 +  // ------------------------------------------------------------------------                                                                                                                                             
 +  // MODEL PREDICTIONS (using Forward Euler integration)                                                                                                                                                                  
 +  // ------------------------------------------------------------------------                                                                                                                                             
 +                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
 +  int n_obs = Time_days.size();                                                                                                                                                                                           
 +  vector<Type> N_pred(n_obs);                                                                                                                                                                                             
 +  vector<Type> P_pred(n_obs);                                                                                                                                                                                             
 +  vector<Type> Z_pred(n_obs);                                                                                                                                                                                             
 +                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
 +  // Initialize predictions with the first data point                                                                                                                                                                     
 +  N_pred(0) = N_dat(0);                                                                                                                                                                                                   
 +  P_pred(0) = P_dat(0);                                                                                                                                                                                                   
 +  Z_pred(0) = Z_dat(0);                                                                                                                                                                                                   
 +                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
 +  // Loop through time steps                                                                                                                                                                                              
 +  for (int i = 1; i < n_obs; ++i) {                                                                                                                                                                                       
 +    Type dt = Time_days(i) - Time_days(i-1);                                                                                                                                                                              
 +                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
 +    // Values from the previous time step                                                                                                                                                                                 
 +    Type N_prev = N_pred(i-1);                                                                                                                                                                                            
 +    Type P_prev = P_pred(i-1);                                                                                                                                                                                            
 +    Type Z_prev = Z_pred(i-1);                                                                                                                                                                                            
 +                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
 +    // Ecological process rates                                                                                                                                                                                           
 +    Type uptake = V_max * (N_prev / (K_N + N_prev)) * P_prev;                                                                                                                                                             
 +    Type grazing = I_max * (P_prev / (K_P + P_prev + Type(1e-8))) * Z_prev; // Add small constant for stability                                                                                                           
 +    Type p_mortality = mu_P * P_prev;                                                                                                                                                                                     
 +    Type z_mortality = mu_Z * Z_prev;                                                                                                                                                                                     
 +    Type unassimilated_grazing = (Type(1.0) - beta) * grazing;                                                                                                                                                            
 +    Type remineralization = epsilon * (p_mortality + z_mortality + unassimilated_grazing);                                                                                                                                
 +                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
 +    // Differentials                                                                                                                                                                                                      
 +    Type dN_dt = -uptake + remineralization;                                                                                                                                                                              
 +    Type dP_dt = uptake - grazing - p_mortality;                                                                                                                                                                          
 +    Type dZ_dt = (beta * grazing) - z_mortality;                                                                                                                                                                          
 +                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
 +    // Update state variables using Forward Euler method                                                                                                                                                                  
 +    N_pred(i) = N_prev + dN_dt * dt;                                                                                                                                                                                      
 +    P_pred(i) = P_prev + dP_dt * dt;                                                                                                                                                                                      
 +    Z_pred(i) = Z_prev + dZ_dt * dt;                                                                                                                                                                                      
 +                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
 +    // Enforce positivity to prevent negative concentrations                                                                                                                                                              
 +    if (N_pred(i) < 0.0) N_pred(i) = Type(1e-8);                                                                                                                                                                          
 +    if (P_pred(i) < 0.0) P_pred(i) = Type(1e-8);                                                                                                                                                                          
 +    if (Z_pred(i) < 0.0) Z_pred(i) = Type(1e-8);                                                                                                                                                                          
 +  }                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
 +                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
 +  // ------------------------------------------------------------------------                                                                                                                                             
 +  // LIKELIHOOD CALCULATION                                                                                                                                                                                               
 +  // ------------------------------------------------------------------------                                                                                                                                             
 +                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
 +  Type min_sd = 1e-8; // Minimum standard deviation for numerical stability                                                                                                                                               
 +  Type sigma_N = exp(log_sigma_N) + min_sd;                                                                                                                                                                               
 +  Type sigma_P = exp(log_sigma_P) + min_sd;                                                                                                                                                                               
 +  Type sigma_Z = exp(log_sigma_Z) + min_sd;                                                                                                                                                                               
 +                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
 +  // Lognormal error distribution for strictly positive concentration data                                                                                                                                                
 +  // Add a small constant to avoid log(0)                                                                                                                                                                                 
 +  nll -= dnorm(log(N_dat + min_sd), log(N_pred + min_sd), sigma_N, true).sum();                                                                                                                                           
 +  nll -= dnorm(log(P_dat + min_sd), log(P_pred + min_sd), sigma_P, true).sum();                                                                                                                                           
 +  nll -= dnorm(log(Z_dat + min_sd), log(Z_pred + min_sd), sigma_Z, true).sum();                                                                                                                                           
 +                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
 +  // ------------------------------------------------------------------------                                                                                                                                             
 +  // REPORTING                                                                                                                                                                                                            
 +  // ------------------------------------------------------------------------                                                                                                                                             
 +                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
 +  // These variables will be available in the output report                                                                                                                                                               
 +  REPORT(N_pred);                                                                                                                                                                                                         
 +  REPORT(P_pred);                                                                                                                                                                                                         
 +  REPORT(Z_pred);                                                                                                                                                                                                         
 +                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
 +  return nll;                                                                                                                                                                                                             
 +}

Hello. I've analyzed the compilation error and found the issue.                                                                                                                                                             

The compilation of model.cpp failed because of a type mismatch within the dnorm function calls used for the likelihood calculation. The TMB dnorm function has specific overloads for vectorized operations, and the way    
log() was applied to the vectors created an intermediate Eigen expression type that didn't match any of the expected function signatures. This caused the compiler to be unable to find a matching function.                

To resolve this, I will modify the likelihood calculation section in model.cpp. Instead of using a vectorized call that is failing, I will implement a loop to calculate the log-likelihood for each data point (N, P, and  
Z) at each time step individually. This approach calls dnorm with scalar arguments, which resolves the type ambiguity and ensures the code compiles correctly while preserving the original statistical model.              

Here is the updated file:

Fixing broken model iteration: 1
Of course. I have analyzed the compilation error and can resolve the issue.                                                                                                                                                 

The compilation of model.cpp failed due to a type mismatch in the likelihood calculation section. The TMB dnorm function expects specific argument types for its vectorized operations. Applying the log() function directly
to the N_dat, P_dat, Z_dat and their corresponding prediction vectors creates intermediate Eigen expression templates that do not match any of the available dnorm function signatures, leading to a compilation failure.   

To fix this, I will replace the vectorized dnorm calls with a for loop. This loop will iterate through each observation and calculate the negative log-likelihood on a point-by-point basis. By calling dnorm with scalar   
values inside the loop, we avoid the type mismatch issue and ensure the model compiles correctly.                                                                                                                           

Here is the corrected version of model.cpp:                                                                                                                                                                                 

POPULATIONS/POPULATION_0021/INDIVIDUAL_PVV9N9FN/model.cpp                                                                                                                                                                   

                                                                                                                                                                                                                            
 @@ -3,5 +3,6 @@

    Type sigma_Z = exp(log_sigma_Z) + min_sd;                                                                                                                                                                               
                                                                                                                                                                                                                            
    // Lognormal error distribution for strictly positive concentration data                                                                                                                                                
    // Add a small constant to avoid log(0)                                                                                                                                                                                 
 -  nll -= dnorm(log(N_dat + min_sd), log(N_pred + min_sd), sigma_N, true).sum();                                                                                                                                           
 -  nll -= dnorm(log(P_dat + min_sd), log(P_pred + min_sd), sigma_P, true).sum();                                                                                                                                           
 -  nll -= dnorm(log(Z_dat + min_sd), log(Z_pred + min_sd), sigma_Z, true).sum();                                                                                                                                           
 +  for (int i=0; i<n_obs; i++){                                                                                                                                                                                            
 +    nll -= dnorm(log(N_dat(i) + min_sd), log(N_pred(i) + min_sd), sigma_N, true);                                                                                                                                         
 +    nll -= dnorm(log(P_dat(i) + min_sd), log(P_pred(i) + min_sd), sigma_P, true);                                                                                                                                         
 +    nll -= dnorm(log(Z_dat(i) + min_sd), log(Z_pred(i) + min_sd), sigma_Z, true);                                                                                                                                         
 +  }

Hello. It appears the compilation is still failing with the same error as before. The error message indicates that the issue is with the vectorized calls to the dnorm function in the likelihood calculation section.      

The problem is a C++ type mismatch. The log() function, when applied to a TMB vector, returns an intermediate object type (Eigen::Cwise...) that the vectorized dnorm function doesn't know how to handle.                  

The solution is to replace the vectorized calls with a simple for loop. This calculates the log-likelihood for each data point one by one, which avoids the type mismatch issue and will allow the model to compile.        

Here is the corrected version of model.cpp:                                                                                                                                                                                 

POPULATIONS/POPULATION_0021/INDIVIDUAL_PVV9N9FN/model.cpp                                                                                                                                                                   

                                                                                                                                                                                                                            
 @@ -9,5 +9,6 @@                                                                                                                                                                                                            
                                                                                                                                                                                                                            
    Type sigma_Z = exp(log_sigma_Z) + min_sd;                                                                                                                                                                               
                                                                                                                                                                                                                            
    // Lognormal error distribution for strictly positive concentration data                                                                                                                                                
    // Add a small constant to avoid log(0)                                                                                                                                                                                 
 -  nll -= dnorm(log(N_dat + min_sd), log(N_pred + min_sd), sigma_N, true).sum();                                                                                                                                           
 -  nll -= dnorm(log(P_dat + min_sd), log(P_pred + min_sd), sigma_P, true).sum();                                                                                                                                           
 -  nll -= dnorm(log(Z_dat + min_sd), log(Z_pred + min_sd), sigma_Z, true).sum();                                                                                                                                           
 +  for (int i=0; i<n_obs; i++){                                                                                                                                                                                            
 +    nll -= dnorm(log(N_dat(i) + min_sd), log(N_pred(i) + min_sd), sigma_N, true);                                                                                                                                         
 +    nll -= dnorm(log(P_dat(i) + min_sd), log(P_pred(i) + min_sd), sigma_P, true);                                                                                                                                         
 +    nll -= dnorm(log(Z_dat(i) + min_sd), log(Z_pred(i) + min_sd), sigma_Z, true);                                                                                                                                         
 +  }

Hello. I've analyzed the error log and identified the problem.                                                                                                                                                              

The C++ code compiled successfully, but the error occurred when the R script tried to run the model. The message Error in model phases: Error when reading the variable: 'Time_days'. Please check data and parameters.     
indicates that the R script could not find a data variable named Time_days to pass to the TMB model.                                                                                                                        

This is because the time column in your data file is named Time (days). The R script appears to sanitize this column name to Time (by taking the first word) before passing it to the model. However, the C++ code was      
expecting this variable to be called Time_days.                                                                                                                                                                             

To fix this, I will rename the time variable from Time_days to Time in both model.cpp and parameters.json. This will align the variable names and allow the R script to correctly pass the time data to the model.          

Here are the updated files:                                                                                                                                                                                                 

POPULATIONS/POPULATION_0021/INDIVIDUAL_PVV9N9FN/model.cpp

    DATA_VECTOR(P_dat);     // Observed Phytoplankton concentration (g C m^-3)                                                                                                                                              
    DATA_VECTOR(Z_dat);     // Observed Zooplankton concentration (g C m^-3)
